nearly complete record of all students of the georgaugustuniversitaet goettingen 26092008 27092008 the following data has been extraced from worldreadable ldap server belonging to the university of goettingen the server is controlled by studit the leak has been open for at least half year and as far as we have been told studit has been informed about it month ago as it has not been closed we will now publish sample data with masked surnames and account uids from accounts with account number greater than 1000000 though you will be able to load complete record from himurostudunigoettingendeldap the data on himuro itself contains only pre and surname and the email address which is the same as the account name by the way there has also been leak for all passwords in flexnow which should be closed by now if you are student at the university of goettingen please update your password and get informed greetings marten s greedy workgroup student data following
